(function () {

    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🛠️ [SECTION] GLOBAL KNOBS (EASILY EDITABLE)
    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var DEBUG = 0;               // 0 = Silent | 1 = Show [Emotion] text & Console Logs
    var APPLY_LIMIT = 6;         // Cap total applied entries (main entries + triggers + shifts)
    var MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY = 1; // Max number of Shifts that can apply per dynamicLore entry (1 = best-match only)

    var EMOTION_THRESHOLD = 0.35; // Min prob to register a mood keyword (e.g., user.mood.angry)
    var SUBTEXT_THRESHOLD = 0.55; // Min prob to register a subtext keyword (e.g., bot.subtext.mocking)
    var MAX_EMOTIONS = 2;        // Only register top N emotions per source (currently unused in sorting)

    // NEW: parity knob with ORBIT – lets you kill *all* keyword/recency/cooldown gates
    var ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES = 1; // 1 = full heuristics on | 0 = purely condition/CNN-driven

    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 📚 [SECTION] DYNAMIC LORE DATA (USER CONTENT)
    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    /*
    This is where you define your lore entries. Each entry is an object that can
    influence the character's persona and scenario context.

    --- ENTRY STRUCTURE ---
    {
        // 1. **ACTIVATION GATES**
        //    Define what must be true for this entry to be considered.
        
        //   A. Keyword-based Activation (Last Message from User or Char):
        //      - `keywords`: Array of strings OR object `{any: [], all: []}`
        //        Example: `keywords: ["hello", "goodbye"]` OR 
        //                 `keywords: { any: ["test"], all: ["all*"] }` 
        //                 (use '*' for word start matching: 'all*' matches 'allure', 'allow', etc.)

        //   B. Probabilistic Condition-based Activation (Best Accuracy):
        //      - `condition`: String expression for checking CNN-inferred probabilities.
        //        * Syntax: `(user.mood.angry_irritated || bot.subtext.polite_indirect_hint) && scene.mood.calm`
        //        * Full list of possible terms can be found in the global `user`, `bot`, and `scene` objects.
        //        * **Moods (user/bot/scene.mood):**
        //          neutral, calm_relaxed, content_warm, happy_joyful, excited_thrilled,
        //          sad_hurt, anxious_worried, angry_irritated, confused_uncertain,
        //          surprised, disgusted_repulsed, afraid_scared.
        //        * **Subtexts (user/bot/scene.subtext):**
        //          agreement_confirmation, polite_indirect_hint, passive_aggressive,
        //          mocking_derisive, hidden_vulnerability, defensive_justifying,
        //          dominating_demanding, submissive_apologetic, formal_reserved,
        //          informal_casual.
        //        * **NEW SEMANTICS (parity with ORBIT):**
        //          - `&&` uses the weakest link:   P(A && B) = min(P(A), P(B))
        //          - `||` uses the strongest link: P(A || B) = max(P(A), P(B))

        //   C. Contextual Gates:
        //      - `minMessages`/`maxMessages`: Only activate between these chat message counts (inclusive).
        //      - `probability`: Float [0, 1] or "X%" string (e.g., 0.5 or "50%") chance to pass gate.
        //      - `nameBlock`: Array of normalized character names to block activation for.
        //      - `speaker`: "user" or "char" - must match the speaker of the *last* message.
        //      - `recency`: Integer N. Requires at least one keyword in the last N messages.
        //      - `cooldown`: Integer N. Prevents entry from activating if a keyword in its text
        //        is too similar to recent chat history. Use sparingly.
        //
        //      - **NEW (parity with ORBIT)**
        //        - `conditionOnly: true` → skip keyword/recency/cooldown gates entirely
        //          and rely purely on CNN conditions (mood/subtext tree).

        // 2. **EFFECTS & PRIORITY**
        //    - `priority`: Number (Default 3). Higher number = evaluated first for sorting.
        //    - `tag`: The tag this entry *responds* to (for triggered entries only).
        //    - `triggers`: Array of strings. Tags this entry will set if it activates.
        //    - `personality`: String added to character's personality/memory.
        //    - `scenario`: String added to character's scenario/context.

        // 3. **SHIFTS (Conditional Overrides)**
        //    - `Shifts`: Array of shift objects. A Shift is a sub-entry that can override the
        //      main entry's `personality`/`scenario` *if* its gates/conditions pass. 
        //      The single Shift with the highest probability is applied
        //      (controlled by MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY knob).
    // }
    */
    // 🟢🟢🟢 SAFE TO EDIT BELOW THIS LINE 🟢🟢🟢
    var dynamicLore = [
        // --- EXAMPLE ENTRY: Keyword Match ---
        {
            keywords: ["test me"],
            personality: "The character is currently observing the user's reaction carefully."
        },
        // --- EXAMPLE ENTRY: Condition Match ---
        {
            condition: "user.mood.angry_irritated && bot.subtext.polite_indirect_hint",
            priority: 5, // High priority
            scenario: "The character is masking their internal irritation with excessive politeness."
        },
        // --- EXAMPLE ENTRY: Shifts ---
        {
            keywords: ["apologize"],
            scenario: "The character acknowledges the user's apology with a reserved nod.",
            Shifts: [
                {
                    // This shift only happens if the bot is also angry
                    condition: "bot.mood.angry_irritated",
                    personality: "The character is still visibly upset and doesn't fully accept the apology yet."
                },
                {
                    // This is the fallback shift if the condition above is false
                    // NOTE: Shift with no condition/keywords is the default.
                    personality: "The character accepts the apology and feels a sense of relief."
                }
            ]
        },
        // --- EXAMPLE ENTRY: Triggered Entry (Passive) ---
        {
            tag: "initial_conflict",
            priority: 1, // Low priority (as it's background context)
            scenario: "The tension from the initial conflict lingers in the air."
        },
        // --- EXAMPLE ENTRY: Entry that sets a Trigger ---
        {
            keywords: ["fight", "conflict"],
            triggers: ["initial_conflict"],
            probability: 0.7,
            scenario: "A new conflict has been detected."
        }
    ];

    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    //## 🔎 [SECTION] PRE-DEFINED KEYWORD GROUPS
    // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var words = {
        jealous: ["jealous", "envy", "envious", "possessive", "territorial", "protective", "insecure", "threatened", "uneasy", "clingy", "guarded", "sharp", "prickly"],
        challenge: ["challenge", "challenges", "challenged", "test", "tests", "tested", "dare", "dares", "dared", "tease", "teases", "teased", "prod", "prods", "push", "pushes", "provoke", "provokes"],
        apology: ["apology", "apologize", "apologizes", "apologized", "sorry", "mend", "mends", "repair", "repairs", "fix", "fixes", "regret", "regrets", "makeup", "reconcile"],
        comfort: ["reassure", "reassures", "comfort", "comforts", "soothe", "soothes", "soften", "softens", "steady", "steadies", "calm", "calms", "support", "supports", "validate", "validates"],
        touch: ["hug", "hugs", "hold", "holds", "touch", "touches", "lean", "leans", "sit", "sits", "brush", "brushes", "rest", "rests", "bump", "bumps", "nudge", "nudges", "squeeze", "cling", "cuddle"],
        practical_care: ["tired", "hungry", "thirsty", "water", "snack", "break", "rest", "sleep", "overwhelmed", "headache", "dizzy", "breathe", "overworked", "burnout"],
        de_escalate: ["argue", "argument", "fight", "conflict", "drama", "tension", "heated", "escalate", "shouting", "blowup"],
        negative: ["frowns", "sighs", "angry", "glares", "pout", "upset", "worried", "sad", "cries", "hurt", "anxious", "panic", "tense", "cold", "mad"],
        observe: ["stare", "stares", "stared", "watch", "watches", "watched", "watching", "observe", "observes", "observing", "quiet", "silence", "silent", "still", "calm", "hushed"],
        comparison: ["better", "worse", "best", "least", "more", "less", "greater", "fewer", "higher", "lower", "above", "below", "rank", "ranks", "ranked", "compare", "versus", "vs"],
        loyalty: ["promise", "promised", "vow", "commit", "commitment", "trust", "loyal", "loyalty", "show up", "follow through"],
        praise: ["praise", "praises", "compliment", "compliments", "complimented", "believe", "believes", "admire", "admires", "admired", "encourage", "encourages"],
        withdraw: ["withdraw", "withdraws", "pull", "pulls", "avoid", "avoids", "turn", "turns", "retreat", "retreats", "shrink", "shrinks", "flinch", "flinches", "recoil", "distance"]
    };
    // 🛑🛑🛑 DO NOT EDIT BELOW THIS LINE 🛑🛑🛑

    /* ============================================================================
    [SECTION] SAFETY / HOST GUARDS
    ========================================================================== */
    if (typeof context !== "object" || !context) return;
    if (typeof context.chat !== "object" || !context.chat) return;
    context.character = context.character || {};
    if (!context.character.scenario) context.character.scenario = "";

    function safeLog(msg) {
        if (!DEBUG) return;
        try {
            if (typeof console !== "undefined" && typeof console.log === "function") {
                console.log(msg);
            }
        } catch (e) { }
    }

    /* ============================================================================
    [SECTION] CNN MODEL PAYLOAD
    ========================================================================= */
    let MODEL = null;
    let MODEL_INIT_ERROR = false;
    const MAX_TOKENS = 48;

    function prettyLabel(raw) { return (raw || "").replace(/_/g, " "); }
    function cnn_labelToWord(raw) { return String(raw || "").toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, ""); }

    // -------------------------- CNN INIT -----------------------------
    function initModel() {
        if (MODEL || MODEL_INIT_ERROR) return;
        var rawData = "";
        try {
            rawData = getRawModelData();
        } catch (err) {
            safeLog("[Subtext] Hoisting Access Failed: " + err.message);
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            return;
        }
        if (!rawData || rawData.length < 50) {
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            safeLog("[Subtext] Model Load Failed: String is empty or too short. Check the bottom of the script.");
            return;
        }
        let parsed;
        try {
            parsed = JSON.parse(rawData);
        } catch (e) {
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            safeLog("[Subtext] JSON Parse Error. Check for broken quotes/commas in the model string.");
            return;
        }
        try {
            const w = parsed.weights || {};
            const s = parsed.scales || {};
            function deq(intList, scale) {
                if (!intList || scale == null) return null;
                const out = new Float32Array(intList.length);
                for (let i = 0; i < intList.length; i++) out[i] = intList[i] * scale;
                return out;
            }
            const convs = [];
            const numConvs = parsed.num_convs || 3;
            const KERNEL_SIZES = [3, 4, 5];
            for (let i = 0; i < numConvs; i++) {
                convs.push({
                    w: deq(w["c" + i + "w"], s["c" + i + "w"]),
                    b: deq(w["c" + i + "b"], s["c" + i + "b"]),
                    k: KERNEL_SIZES[i] || 3
                });
            }
            let vocabList = [];
            let vocabMap = {};
            if (Array.isArray(parsed.vocab)) {
                vocabList = parsed.vocab.slice();
                for (let i = 0; i < vocabList.length; i++) {
                    vocabMap[vocabList[i]] = i;
                }
            } else {
                vocabMap = parsed.vocab || {};
                vocabList = Object.keys(vocabMap).sort(function (a, b) {
                    return vocabMap[a] - vocabMap[b];
                });
            }
            let unkId = vocabMap[parsed.unk_token || "<unk>"];
            if (unkId == null || !isFinite(unkId)) unkId = 0;
            MODEL = {
                vocab: vocabList,
                vocabMap: vocabMap,
                vocabSize: parsed.vocab_size || vocabList.length,
                embedDim: parsed.embed_dim || 16,
                numConvs: numConvs,
                numEmo: parsed.num_emo_labels || (parsed.emotion_classes || []).length,
                numSub: parsed.num_labels || (parsed.subtext_classes || []).length,
                unkId: unkId,
                embedding: deq(w.emb, s.emb),
                convs: convs,
                emoW: deq(w.ew, s.ew),
                emoB: deq(w.eb, s.eb),
                subW: deq(w.sw, s.sw),
                subB: deq(w.sb, s.sb),
                emotionLabels: parsed.emotion_classes || [],
                subtextLabels: parsed.subtext_classes || []
            };
            safeLog("[Subtext] Init success.");
        } catch (e) {
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            safeLog("[Subtext] Init error: " + e.message);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------- CNN INFERENCE ----------------------------------
    function cnn_tokenize(text) {
        return (text || "").toLowerCase()
            .replace(/([?.!,])/g, " $1 ")
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s?.!,]/g, " ")
            .trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).slice(0, MAX_TOKENS);
    }

    function conv1d_max_relu(inputCHW, weight, bias, C, L, k) {
        if (!weight || !bias) return new Float32Array(0);
        const O = (weight.length / (C * k)) | 0;
        const out = new Float32Array(O);
        const pad = (k - 1) >> 1;
        for (let f = 0; f < O; f++) {
            let mx = -Infinity;
            const wOff = f * C * k;
            for (let t = 0; t < L; t++) {
                let sum = bias[f];
                const base = C * t;
                const wBase = wOff;
                for (let c = 0; c < C; c++) {
                    for (let j = 0; j < k; j++) {
                        const idx = t + j - pad;
                        if (idx >= 0 && idx < L) {
                            const inIdx = c * L + idx;
                            const wIdx = wBase + c * k + j;
                            sum += inputCHW[inIdx] * weight[wIdx];
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (sum > mx) mx = sum;
            }
            out[f] = mx > 0 ? mx : 0;
        }
        return out;
    }

    function applyHeuristics(emoProbs, subProbs) {
        if (!MODEL) return;
        const eL = MODEL.emotionLabels, sL = MODEL.subtextLabels;
        const idx = (arr, val) => arr.indexOf(val);

        // 1. Masking
        const iVuln = idx(sL, "hidden_vulnerability");
        if (iVuln >= 0 && subProbs[iVuln] > 0.60) {
            safeLog("[Heuristic] Masking: Suppressing positive emotions.");
            ["neutral", "content_warm", "happy_joyful"].forEach(k => {
                const i = idx(eL, k); if (i >= 0) emoProbs[i] *= 0.1;
            });
        }
        // 2. Passive Aggressive
        const iAngry = idx(eL, "angry_irritated"),
              iPolite = idx(sL, "polite_indirect_hint"),
              iPass = idx(sL, "passive_aggressive");
        if (iAngry >= 0 && iPolite >= 0 && iPass >= 0 &&
            emoProbs[iAngry] > 0.4 && subProbs[iPolite] > 0.4) {
            safeLog("[Heuristic] Passive Aggressive: Boosting subtext.");
            subProbs[iPass] = Math.max(subProbs[iPass], 0.95);
            subProbs[iPolite] *= 0.2;
        }
        // 3. Sarcasm
        const iMock = idx(sL, "mocking_derisive");
        if (iMock >= 0 && subProbs[iMock] > 0.50) {
            safeLog("[Heuristic] Sarcasm: Killing joy.");
            ["happy_joyful", "excited_thrilled"].forEach(k => {
                const i = idx(eL, k); if (i >= 0 && emoProbs[i] < subProbs[iMock]) emoProbs[i] = 0;
            });
        }
        // 4. Neutral Cleanup
        const iNeut = idx(eL, "neutral");
        if (iNeut >= 0 && emoProbs[iNeut] > 0) {
            let maxOther = 0;
            for (let i = 0; i < emoProbs.length; i++) {
                if (i !== iNeut && emoProbs[i] > maxOther) maxOther = emoProbs[i];
            }
            if (maxOther > 0.65) emoProbs[iNeut] = 0;
        }
    }

    function cnn_predict(text) {
        initModel();
        if (!MODEL) return null;
        const tokens = cnn_tokenize(text);
        const ids = tokens.map(function (t) {
            var id = MODEL.vocabMap[t];
            return (typeof id === "number") ? id : MODEL.unkId;
        });
        while (ids.length < MAX_TOKENS) ids.push(0);
        if (ids.length > MAX_TOKENS) ids.length = MAX_TOKENS;

        const T = MAX_TOKENS, C = MODEL.embedDim;
        const embeddedCHW = new Float32Array(C * T);
        for (let t = 0; t < T; t++) {
            const id = ids[t];
            if (id < MODEL.vocabSize) {
                const srcOff = id * C;
                for (let c = 0; c < C; c++) embeddedCHW[c * T + t] = MODEL.embedding[srcOff + c];
            }
        }

        const convOutputs = MODEL.convs.map(c => conv1d_max_relu(embeddedCHW, c.w, c.b, C, T, c.k));
        const featSize = convOutputs.reduce((a, b) => a + b.length, 0);
        const feats = new Float32Array(featSize);
        let off = 0;
        convOutputs.forEach(o => { feats.set(o, off); off += o.length; });

        function forwardHead(w, b, n) {
            const outLogits = new Float32Array(n);
            let maxLogit = -Infinity;
            for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
                let sum = b[i];
                const wOff = i * featSize;
                for (let j = 0; j < featSize; j++) sum += w[wOff + j] * feats[j];
                outLogits[i] = sum;
                if (sum > maxLogit) maxLogit = sum;
            }
            return { logits: outLogits, maxLogit: maxLogit };
        }

        const eRes = forwardHead(MODEL.emoW, MODEL.emoB, MODEL.numEmo);
        let eSum = 0;
        const emoProbs = new Array(MODEL.numEmo);
        for (let i = 0; i < MODEL.numEmo; i++) {
            const e = Math.exp(eRes.logits[i] - eRes.maxLogit);
            emoProbs[i] = e; eSum += e;
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < MODEL.numEmo; i++) emoProbs[i] /= (eSum || 1);

        const sRes = forwardHead(MODEL.subW, MODEL.subB, MODEL.numSub);
        const subProbs = new Array(MODEL.numSub);
        for (let i = 0; i < MODEL.numSub; i++) subProbs[i] = 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-sRes.logits[i]));

        applyHeuristics(emoProbs, subProbs);
        return { emo: emoProbs, sub: subProbs };
    }

    function filterTopResults(probs, labels, threshold, limit) {
        if (!probs || !labels) return [];
        return labels.map((l, i) => ({ label: l, prob: probs[i] || 0 }))
            .filter(item => item.prob >= threshold)
            .sort((a, b) => b.prob - a.prob)
            .slice(0, limit);
    }

    /* ============================================================================
        [SECTION] KEYWORD GENERATION & INPUT PROCESSING (Hybrid Tree v2)
        ========================================================================== */
    const msgs = (context.chat && context.chat.last_messages) || [];

    const normalize = (str) => (str || '').toLowerCase()
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9_\s-]/g, " ")
        .replace(/[-_]+/g, " ")
        .replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();

    const rawLastMsg = msgs.at(-1)?.message || "";
    const rawPrevMsg = msgs.at(-2)?.message || "";
    const rawScene = msgs.slice(-6).map(m => m.message || "").join(" ");

    const normLastMsg = normalize(rawLastMsg);

    var user = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };
    var bot = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };
    var scene = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };

    var CNN_KEYWORDS = "";

    (function () {
        try {
            if (typeof cnn_predict !== "function") return;
            var resUser = rawLastMsg ? cnn_predict(rawLastMsg) : null;
            var resBot = rawPrevMsg ? cnn_predict(rawPrevMsg) : null;
            var resScene = rawScene ? cnn_predict(rawScene) : null;

            function populateTree(targetObj, predictionResult) {
                if (!predictionResult) return;
                filterTopResults(predictionResult.emo, MODEL.emotionLabels, 0.1, MAX_EMOTIONS).forEach(item => {
                    let key = item.label;
                    let simpleKey = key.split('_')[0];
                    targetObj.mood[key] = item.prob;
                    if (key !== simpleKey) targetObj.mood[simpleKey] = item.prob;
                });
                filterTopResults(predictionResult.sub, MODEL.subtextLabels, 0.1, 99).forEach(item => {
                    let key = item.label;
                    let simpleKey = key.split('_')[0];
                    targetObj.subtext[key] = item.prob;
                    if (key !== simpleKey) targetObj.subtext[simpleKey] = item.prob;
                });
            }

            if (MODEL) {
                populateTree(user, resUser);
                populateTree(bot, resBot);
                populateTree(scene, resScene);
            }

            var kw = [];
            function pushLegacyKw(sourceStr, targetObj) {
                for (let k in targetObj.mood) {
                    if (targetObj.mood[k] >= EMOTION_THRESHOLD) kw.push(sourceStr + ".mood." + k);
                }
                for (let k in targetObj.subtext) {
                    if (targetObj.subtext[k] >= SUBTEXT_THRESHOLD) kw.push(sourceStr + ".subtext." + k);
                }
            }
            pushLegacyKw("user", user);
            pushLegacyKw("char", bot);
            pushLegacyKw("scene", scene);
            CNN_KEYWORDS = kw.join(" ");
            if (DEBUG) safeLog("[Keywords]: " + CNN_KEYWORDS);

            if (DEBUG) {
                function pretty(obj, title) {
                    let es = Object.keys(obj.mood).sort((a, b) => obj.mood[b] - obj.mood[a]).slice(0, 2)
                        .map(k => k + " " + Math.round(obj.mood[k] * 100) + "%").join(", ");
                    let ss = Object.keys(obj.subtext).sort((a, b) => obj.subtext[b] - obj.subtext[a]).slice(0, 2)
                        .map(k => k + " " + Math.round(obj.subtext[k] * 100) + "%").join(", ");
                    context.character.scenario += "\n\n[" + title + "]\n[Emotion]: " + (es || "neutral") + "\n[Subtext]: " + (ss || "none");
                }
                pretty(user, "User Analysis");
                pretty(bot, "Char Analysis");
                pretty(scene, "Scene Analysis");
            }
        } catch (e) { safeLog("[Logic Error]: " + e.message); }
    })();

    var last = " " + normLastMsg + " " + normalize(CNN_KEYWORDS) + " ";

    /* ============================================================================
        [SECTION] CORE LORE LOGIC & GATES
        ========================================================================== */
    var _norm = normalize;
    var messageCount = (msgs.length) || (context.chat && context.chat.message_count) || 0;
    var activeName = _norm((context.character && context.character.name) || "");

    function arr(x) { return Array.isArray(x) ? x : (x == null ? [] : [x]); }

    function collectWordGates(e) {
        var r = (e && e.requires) ? e.requires : {};
        var any = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireAny), arr(e && e.andAny), arr(r.any));
        var all = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireAll), arr(e && e.andAll), arr(r.all));
        var none = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireNone), arr(e && e.notAny), arr(e && e.block), arr(r.none));
        var nall = [].concat(arr(e && e.notAll));
        return { any: any, all: all, none: none, nall: nall };
    }

    function tagsPass(e, activeTagsSet) {
        var anyT = arr(e && e.andAnyTags);
        var allT = arr(e && e.andAllTags);
        var noneT = arr(e && e.notAnyTags);
        var nallT = arr(e && e.notAllTags);
        var hasT = function (t) { return !!activeTagsSet && activeTagsSet[String(t)] === 1; };
        if (anyT.length && !anyT.some(hasT)) return false;
        if (allT.length && !allT.every(hasT)) return false;
        if (noneT.length && noneT.some(hasT)) return false;
        if (nallT.length && nallT.every(hasT)) return false;
        return true;
    }

    // UPDATED: parity with ORBIT's hasTerm (supports '*', underscores, hyphens, digits)
    function hasTerm(hay, term) {
        var t = (term == null ? "" : String(term)).toLowerCase().trim();
        if (!t) return false;
        var esc = t.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, "\\$&");
        if (t.charAt(t.length - 1) === "*") {
            return new RegExp("(?:^|\\s)" + esc.slice(0, -1) + "[a-z0-9_\\-]*?(?=\\s|$)", "i").test(hay);
        }
        return new RegExp("(?:^|\\s)" + esc + "(?=\\s|$)", "i").test(hay);
    }

    function checkKeywords(entry) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        var kw = entry && entry.keywords;
        if (!kw) return false;
        if (Array.isArray(kw)) return kw.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); });
        var any = Array.isArray(kw.any) ? kw.any : [];
        var all = Array.isArray(kw.all) ? kw.all : [];
        if (!any.length && !all.length) return false;
        if (any.length && !any.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        if (all.length && !all.every(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        return true;
    }

    // --- SMART CONDITION CHECKER (parity with ORBIT: AND=min, OR=max) ---
    function checkCondition(e) {
        if (!e || !e.condition) return 0;

        function getPathProb(pathStr) {
            var parts = String(pathStr).trim().split(".");
            if (!parts.length) return 0;
            var rootName = parts[0];
            var root = rootName === "user" ? user :
                (rootName === "bot" ? bot :
                    (rootName === "scene" ? scene : null));
            if (!root) return 0;
            var val = root;
            for (var i = 1; i < parts.length; i++) {
                val = val ? val[parts[i]] : undefined;
                if (val == null) break;
            }
            var num = (typeof val === "number" && val > 0) ? val : 0;
            return num;
        }

        if (typeof e.condition === "function") {
            return e.condition(user, bot, scene) ? 1 : 0;
        }
        if (typeof e.condition !== "string") return 0;
        var expr = e.condition.trim();
        if (!expr) return 0;

        // Fast-path AND only (no OR/parens)
        if (expr.indexOf("||") === -1 && expr.indexOf("(") === -1 && expr.indexOf(")") === -1) {
            var andTerms = expr.split("&&").map(function (t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(Boolean);
            if (!andTerms.length) return 0;
            var prob = 1.0;
            for (var i = 0; i < andTerms.length; i++) {
                var p = getPathProb(andTerms[i]);
                if (p === 0) return 0;
                if (p < prob) prob = p; // AND = weakest link
            }
            return prob;
        }

        var tokens = expr.match(/[\w.]+|&&|\|\||[()]/g) || [];
        if (!tokens.length) return 0;

        var output = [];
        var ops = [];
        function prec(op) {
            if (op === "&&") return 2;
            if (op === "||") return 1;
            return 0;
        }
        function isOp(t) { return t === "&&" || t === "||"; }

        for (var ti = 0; ti < tokens.length; ti++) {
            var tok = tokens[ti];
            if (tok === "(") {
                ops.push(tok);
            } else if (tok === ")") {
                while (ops.length && ops[ops.length - 1] !== "(") {
                    output.push(ops.pop());
                }
                if (ops.length && ops[ops.length - 1] === "(") ops.pop();
            } else if (isOp(tok)) {
                while (ops.length && isOp(ops[ops.length - 1]) &&
                    prec(ops[ops.length - 1]) >= prec(tok)) {
                    output.push(ops.pop());
                }
                ops.push(tok);
            } else {
                output.push(tok);
            }
        }
        while (ops.length) output.push(ops.pop());

        var stack = [];
        for (var pi = 0; pi < output.length; pi++) {
            var t = output[pi];
            if (!isOp(t)) {
                stack.push(getPathProb(t));
            } else {
                var bProb = stack.length ? stack.pop() : 0;
                var aProb = stack.length ? stack.pop() : 0;
                var res = 0;
                if (t === "&&") {
                    res = Math.min(aProb, bProb); // AND = weakest link
                } else if (t === "||") {
                    res = Math.max(aProb, bProb); // OR = strongest link
                }
                stack.push(res);
            }
        }
        return stack.length ? stack[0] : 0;
    }

    function getMin(e) { return (e && isFinite(e.minMessages)) ? +e.minMessages : -Infinity; }
    function getMax(e) { return (e && isFinite(e.maxMessages)) ? +e.maxMessages : Infinity; }

    function parseProbability(v) {
        if (v == null) return 1;
        if (typeof v === "number") return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
        var s = String(v).trim().toLowerCase();
        var n = parseFloat(s.replace("%", ""));
        if (!isFinite(n)) return 1;
        return s.indexOf("%") !== -1 ? Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n / 100)) : Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n));
    }

    function getNameBlock(e) { return (e && Array.isArray(e.nameBlock)) ? e.nameBlock.slice(0) : []; }

    function isNameBlocked(e) {
        if (!activeName) return false;
        var nb = getNameBlock(e);
        for (var i = 0; i < nb.length; i++) {
            var n = _norm(nb[i]);
            if (!n) continue;
            if (n === activeName) return true;
            if (activeName.indexOf(n) !== -1) return true;
            if (n.indexOf(activeName + " ") === 0) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function getSpeaker() {
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return null;
        var lastMsg = msgs[msgs.length - 1];
        return lastMsg.isUser ? "user" : "char";
    }

    function countKeywordOccurrences(term) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return 0;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return 0;
        var count = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) count++;
        }
        return count;
    }

    function keywordInRecency(term, n) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return false;
        var start = Math.max(0, msgs.length - n);
        for (var i = start; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function keywordAtDepth(term, minDepth, maxDepth) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return false;
        minDepth = (minDepth == null) ? 0 : minDepth;
        maxDepth = (maxDepth == null) ? Infinity : maxDepth;
        for (var i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) {
                var depth = msgs.length - 1 - i;
                if (depth >= minDepth && depth <= maxDepth) return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    function passesCooldown(e) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return true;
        if (!e || !e.cooldown) return true;
        var recentChunk = last || "";
        var tail = msgs.slice(-4);
        for (var i = 0; i < tail.length; i++) {
            recentChunk += " " + (tail[i].message || tail[i].text || "");
        }
        var hash = 0;
        for (var j = 0; j < recentChunk.length; j++) {
            hash = ((hash << 5) - hash + recentChunk.charCodeAt(j)) | 0;
        }
        return (hash & 0x7FFFFFFF) % (e.cooldown + 5) !== 1;
    }

    function keywordTermsFromEntry(e) {
        if (!e || !e.keywords) return [];
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords)) return e.keywords.slice();
        var out = [];
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords.any)) out = out.concat(e.keywords.any);
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords.all)) out = out.concat(e.keywords.all);
        return out;
    }

    function wordGatesPass(e) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return true;

        var g = collectWordGates(e);
        if (g.any.length && !g.any.some(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.all.length && !g.all.every(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.none.length && g.none.some(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.nall.length && g.nall.every(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;

        if (e.keywords && typeof e.keywords === "object" && !Array.isArray(e.keywords)) {
            var any = e.keywords.any || [];
            var all = e.keywords.all || [];
            if (any.length && !any.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
            if (all.length && !all.every(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        }

        var ctxTerms = keywordTermsFromEntry(e);
        if (e.recency !== undefined) {
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return keywordInRecency(t, e.recency); })) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        if (e.frequency !== undefined) {
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return countKeywordOccurrences(t) >= e.frequency; })) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        if (e.depthMin !== undefined || e.depthMax !== undefined) {
            var minD = (e.depthMin == null) ? 0 : e.depthMin;
            var maxD = (e.depthMax == null) ? Infinity : e.depthMax;
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return keywordAtDepth(t, minD, maxD); })) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        if (e.speaker && getSpeaker() !== e.speaker) return false;
        if (!passesCooldown(e)) return false;
        return true;
    }

    function isAlwaysOn(e) {
        var hasKW = !!(e && e.keywords && (Array.isArray(e.keywords) ? e.keywords.length : (e.keywords.any || e.keywords.all)));
        var hasTag = !!(e && e.tag);
        var hasMin = (e && e.minMessages != null);
        var hasMax = (e && e.maxMessages != null);
        var hasCond = !!(e && e.condition);
        return !hasKW && !hasTag && !hasMin && !hasMax && !hasCond;
    }

    function entryPasses(e, activeTagsSet) {
        if (!(messageCount >= getMin(e) && messageCount <= getMax(e))) return false;
        if (isNameBlocked(e)) return false;

        // NEW parity: conditionOnly -> skip keyword/recency/cooldown gates
        var useWordGates = ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES && !(e && e.conditionOnly === true);
        if (useWordGates && !wordGatesPass(e)) return false;

        if (!tagsPass(e, activeTagsSet || {})) return false;
        if (Math.random() > parseProbability(e && e.probability)) return false;
        return true;
    }

    /* ============================================================================
    [SECTION] PROBABILISTIC SORT & APPLICATION
    ========================================================================== */
    var activeTags = {};
    var bufP = "", bufS = "";

    function getEntryProbability(e) {
        var base = 0;

        if (e && e.condition) {
            base = checkCondition(e);
        } else if (checkKeywords(e)) {
            base = 1;
        } else if (isAlwaysOn(e)) {
            base = 1;
        } else {
            base = 0;
        }
        if (!base) return 0;

        var pGate = parseProbability(e && e.probability);
        return base * pGate;
    }

    var picked = [], triggered = [];

    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        var hitProb = getEntryProbability(e);
        if (hitProb > 0 && !e.tag) {
            e._prob = hitProb;
            picked.push(e);
        }
    });

    picked.forEach(function (e) { (e.triggers || []).forEach(function (t) { activeTags[t] = 1; }); });

    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        if (e.tag && activeTags[e.tag]) {
            var hitProb = getEntryProbability(e);
            if (hitProb <= 0 && !e.condition && !e.keywords) {
                hitProb = parseProbability(e && e.probability);
            }
            if (hitProb > 0 && entryPasses(e, activeTags)) {
                e._prob = hitProb;
                triggered.push(e);
            }
        }
    });

    var allActive = [].concat(picked, triggered).filter(function (e, idx, arr) { return arr.indexOf(e) === idx; });

    allActive.sort(function (a, b) {
        var pa = a.priority != null ? a.priority : 3;
        var pb = b.priority != null ? b.priority : 3;
        if (pb !== pa) return pb - pa;
        return (b._prob || 0) - (a._prob || 0);
    });

    var appliedCount = 0;

    allActive.forEach(function (e) {
        if (appliedCount >= APPLY_LIMIT) return;
        if (!entryPasses(e, activeTags)) return;

        if (e.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + e.personality;
        if (e.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + e.scenario;

        if (Array.isArray(e.Shifts)) {
            var shiftsApplied = 0;
            var bestShift = null;
            var maxProb = -1;

            e.Shifts.forEach(function (sh) {
                if (MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY > 0 && shiftsApplied >= MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY) return;

                var shiftProb = 0;
                var match = false;

                if (sh.condition) {
                    shiftProb = checkCondition(sh);
                    if (shiftProb > 0) match = true;
                }

                var hasKW = checkKeywords(sh);
                if (hasKW) {
                    shiftProb = Math.max(shiftProb, sh.condition ? shiftProb : 1);
                    if (shiftProb > 0) match = true;
                } else if (!sh.condition && !hasKW) {
                    match = true;
                    shiftProb = 0.01;
                }

                if (match) {
                    if (!wordGatesPass(sh) || !tagsPass(sh, activeTags) ||
                        isNameBlocked(sh) || Math.random() > parseProbability(sh.probability)) {
                        match = false;
                    }
                }

                if (match && shiftProb > maxProb) {
                    maxProb = shiftProb;
                    bestShift = sh;
                }
            });

            if (bestShift) {
                if (bestShift.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + bestShift.personality;
                if (bestShift.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + bestShift.scenario;
                (bestShift.triggers || []).forEach(function (t) { activeTags[t] = 1; });
                shiftsApplied++;
            }
        }

        appliedCount++;
    });

    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        if (appliedCount >= APPLY_LIMIT) return;
        if (
            e.tag &&
            activeTags[e.tag] &&
            allActive.indexOf(e) === -1 &&
            (checkKeywords(e) || checkCondition(e) > 0 || (!e.condition && !e.keywords))
        ) {
            if (entryPasses(e, activeTags)) {
                if (e.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + e.personality;
                if (e.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + e.scenario;
                appliedCount++;
            }
        }
    });

    if (bufP) context.character.personality += bufP;
    if (bufS) context.character.scenario += bufS;

    /* ============================================================================
        [SECTION] DATA PAYLOAD (HOISTED)
        ========================================================================== */

        // Paste your q-int model JSON here as one big string
